\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}\hypertarget{e1000__82575_8c_ac3d80e08c7b6b2ebe0862db19a042274}{}\label{e1000__82575_8c_ac3d80e08c7b6b2ebe0862db19a042274}
e1000\+\_\+acquire\+\_\+nvm\+\_\+82575 -\/ Request for access to E\+E\+P\+R\+OM \+: pointer to the HW structure

Acquire the necessary semaphores for exclusive access to the E\+E\+P\+R\+OM. Set the E\+E\+P\+R\+OM access request bit and wait for E\+E\+P\+R\+OM access grant bit. Return successful if access grant bit set, else clear the request for E\+E\+P\+R\+OM access and return -\/\+E1000\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+N\+VM (-\/1).

1243     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (data & \hyperlink{kmod_2igb_2e1000__defines_8h_aa3ec8aafe2e3142633a7369ebb8aeff1}{E1000\_M88E1112\_STATUS\_LINK})
1244         port = \hyperlink{kmod_2igb_2e1000__defines_8h_aedd59566aea7431889037b96f396110f}{E1000\_MEDIA\_PORT\_COPPER};
1245 
1246     \textcolor{comment}{/* Check for other. */}
1247     ret\_val = phy->\hyperlink{structe1000__phy__info_a60c9cd1642eed1c082fd37283740fdc9}{ops}.\hyperlink{structe1000__phy__operations_a00dd285f09f84ed5253d2900fd0d8abc}{write\_reg}(hw, \hyperlink{kmod_2igb_2e1000__defines_8h_a4911b4a60ca68f69c3f54ebaec9cce7d}{E1000\_M88E1112\_PAGE\_ADDR}, 1);
1248     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (ret\_val)
1249         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} ret\_val;
1250 
1251     ret\_val = phy->\hyperlink{structe1000__phy__info_a60c9cd1642eed1c082fd37283740fdc9}{ops}.\hyperlink{structe1000__phy__operations_af44e212061c26684f96a0ebad95b082d}{read\_reg}(hw, \hyperlink{kmod_2igb_2e1000__defines_8h_a032c04f00fe2d7d085f018579944e5b9}{E1000\_M88E1112\_STATUS}, &data);
1252     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (ret\_val)
1253         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} ret\_val;
1254 
1255     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (data & E1000\_M88E1112\_STATUS\_LINK)
1256         port = \hyperlink{kmod_2igb_2e1000__defines_8h_a72ecdd464be25f5a1b775789e9bea0f0}{E1000\_MEDIA\_PORT\_OTHER};
1257 
1258     \textcolor{comment}{/* Determine if a swap needs to happen. */}
1259     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (port && (hw->\hyperlink{structe1000__hw_a498aa966bd77b214f1d67900bf6b8236}{dev\_spec}.\hyperlink{structe1000__hw_a65abf35e3ce1758616d7990fdb4d356e}{\_82575}.\hyperlink{structe1000__dev__spec__82575_afad32bd92d6ecd9161275120de8b793d}{media\_port} != port)) \{
1260         hw->\hyperlink{structe1000__hw_a498aa966bd77b214f1d67900bf6b8236}{dev\_spec}.\hyperlink{structe1000__hw_a65abf35e3ce1758616d7990fdb4d356e}{\_82575}.\hyperlink{structe1000__dev__spec__82575_afad32bd92d6ecd9161275120de8b793d}{media\_port} = \hyperlink{gst__avb__playbin_8c_a63c89c04d1feae07ca35558055155ffb}{port};
1261         hw->\hyperlink{structe1000__hw_a498aa966bd77b214f1d67900bf6b8236}{dev\_spec}.\hyperlink{structe1000__hw_a65abf35e3ce1758616d7990fdb4d356e}{\_82575}.\hyperlink{structe1000__dev__spec__82575_ab7ad55be07202708d12927b26dcce99c}{media\_changed} = \textcolor{keyword}{true};
1262     \}
1263 
1264     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (port == \hyperlink{kmod_2igb_2e1000__defines_8h_aedd59566aea7431889037b96f396110f}{E1000\_MEDIA\_PORT\_COPPER}) \{
1265         \textcolor{comment}{/* reset page to 0 */}
1266         ret\_val = phy->\hyperlink{structe1000__phy__info_a60c9cd1642eed1c082fd37283740fdc9}{ops}.\hyperlink{structe1000__phy__operations_a00dd285f09f84ed5253d2900fd0d8abc}{write\_reg}(hw, \hyperlink{kmod_2igb_2e1000__defines_8h_a4911b4a60ca68f69c3f54ebaec9cce7d}{E1000\_M88E1112\_PAGE\_ADDR}, 0);
1267         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (ret\_val)
1268             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} ret\_val;
1269         \hyperlink{e1000__82575_8c_a92f5c080888357f78c9b576712cb35ee}{e1000\_check\_for\_link\_82575}(hw);
1270     \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{
1271         \hyperlink{e1000__82575_8c_a92f5c080888357f78c9b576712cb35ee}{e1000\_check\_for\_link\_82575}(hw);
1272         \textcolor{comment}{/* reset page to 0 */}
1273         ret\_val = phy->\hyperlink{structe1000__phy__info_a60c9cd1642eed1c082fd37283740fdc9}{ops}.\hyperlink{structe1000__phy__operations_a00dd285f09f84ed5253d2900fd0d8abc}{write\_reg}(hw, \hyperlink{kmod_2igb_2e1000__defines_8h_a4911b4a60ca68f69c3f54ebaec9cce7d}{E1000\_M88E1112\_PAGE\_ADDR}, 0);
1274         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (ret\_val)
1275             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} ret\_val;

1277

\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{e1000\+\_\+get\+\_\+cfg\+\_\+done\+\_\+82575(struct e1000\+\_\+hw $\ast$hw)}{e1000_get_cfg_done_82575(struct e1000_hw *hw)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}static {\bf s32} e1000\+\_\+get\+\_\+cfg\+\_\+done\+\_\+82575 (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{struct {\bf e1000\+\_\+hw} $\ast$}]{hw}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}\hypertarget{e1000__82575_8c_a097fa6056a548f6cfcaba75f2c8cdf4d}{}\label{e1000__82575_8c_a097fa6056a548f6cfcaba75f2c8cdf4d}
e1000\+\_\+get\+\_\+cfg\+\_\+done\+\_\+82575 -\/ Read config done bit \+: pointer to the HW structure

Read the management control register for the config done bit for completion status. N\+O\+TE\+: silicon which is E\+E\+P\+R\+O\+M-\/less will fail trying to read the config done bit, so an error is {\itshape O\+N\+LY} logged and returns E1000\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS. If we were to return with error, E\+E\+P\+R\+O\+M-\/less silicon would not be able to be reset or change link. 

e1000\+\_\+82575.\+c 파일의 1122 번째 라인에서 정의되었습니다.

e1000\+\_\+get\+\_\+link\+\_\+up\+\_\+info\+\_\+82575 -\/ Get link speed/duplex info \+: pointer to the HW structure \+: stores the current speed \+: stores the current duplex

This is a wrapper function, if using the serial gigabit media independent interface, use P\+CS to retrieve the link speed and duplex information. Otherwise, use the generic function to get the link speed and duplex info.

\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{struct {\bf e1000\+\_\+hw} $\ast$}]{hw}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}\hypertarget{e1000__82575_8c_aed98314ac26bac32dff26bcb00202ff8}{}\label{e1000__82575_8c_aed98314ac26bac32dff26bcb00202ff8}
e1000\+\_\+get\+\_\+media\+\_\+type\+\_\+82575 -\/ derives current media type. \+: pointer to the HW structure

The media type is chosen reflecting few settings. The following are taken into account\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item link mode set in the current port Init Control Word \#3
\item current link mode settings in C\+SR register
\item M\+D\+IO vs. I2C P\+HY control interface chosen
\item S\+FP module media type 
\end{DoxyItemize}

e1000\+\_\+82575.\+c 파일의 1768 번째 라인에서 정의되었습니다.

e1000\+\_\+get\+\_\+pcs\+\_\+speed\+\_\+and\+\_\+duplex\+\_\+82575 -\/ Retrieve current speed/duplex \+: pointer to the HW structure \+: stores the current speed \+: stores the current duplex

Using the physical coding sub-\/layer (P\+CS), retrieve the current speed and duplex, then store the values in the pointers provided.

e1000\+\_\+get\+\_\+phy\+\_\+id\+\_\+82575 -\/ Retrieve P\+HY addr and id \+: pointer to the HW structure

Retrieves the P\+HY address and ID for both P\+HY\textquotesingle{}s which do and do not use sgmi interface.

1515     ret\_val = mac->\hyperlink{structe1000__mac__info_a6ac57b9c85404edae44f08fe43d7ff02}{ops}.\hyperlink{structe1000__mac__operations_ac8c0c6110e4112267f9b8b7bf1c42b54}{setup\_link}(hw);
1516 
1517     \textcolor{comment}{/* Set the default MTU size */}
1518     hw->\hyperlink{structe1000__hw_a498aa966bd77b214f1d67900bf6b8236}{dev\_spec}.\hyperlink{structe1000__hw_a65abf35e3ce1758616d7990fdb4d356e}{\_82575}.\hyperlink{structe1000__dev__spec__82575_a6bf07cd0dd9e1459d63d3e38c4159bee}{mtu} = 1500;
1519 
1520     \textcolor{comment}{/*}
1521 \textcolor{comment}{     * Clear all of the statistics registers (clear on read).  It is}
1522 \textcolor{comment}{     * important that we do this after we have tried to establish link}
1523 \textcolor{comment}{     * because the symbol error count will increment wildly if there}
1524 \textcolor{comment}{     * is no link.}
1525 \textcolor{comment}{     */}
1526     \hyperlink{e1000__82575_8c_a42dcc0d1bb100de1a4ca83dda7e43ffc}{e1000\_clear\_hw\_cntrs\_82575}(hw);
1527 
1528     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} ret\_val;
1529 \}
\end{DoxyCode}

e1000\+\_\+reset\+\_\+mdicnfg\+\_\+82580 -\/ Reset M\+D\+I\+C\+N\+FG destination and com\+\_\+mdio bits \+: pointer to the HW structure

This resets the the M\+D\+I\+C\+N\+F\+G.\+Destination and M\+D\+I\+C\+N\+F\+G.\+Com\+\_\+\+M\+D\+IO bits based on the values found in the E\+E\+P\+R\+OM. This addresses an issue in which these bits are not restored from E\+E\+P\+R\+OM after reset.

e1000\+\_\+rx\+\_\+fifo\+\_\+flush\+\_\+82575 -\/ Clean rx fifo after Rx enable \+: pointer to the HW structure

After Rx enable, if manageability is enabled then there is likely some bad data at the start of the fifo and possibly in the D\+MA fifo. This function clears the fifos and flushes any packets that came in as rx was being enabled.

e1000\+\_\+rxpbs\+\_\+adjust\+\_\+82580 -\/ adjust R\+X\+P\+BS value to reflect actual Rx P\+BA size \+: data received by reading R\+X\+P\+BS register

The 82580 uses a table based approach for packet buffer allocation sizes. This function converts the retrieved value into the correct table value 0x0 0x1 0x2 0x3 0x4 0x5 0x6 0x7 0x0 36 72 144 1 2 4 8 16 0x8 35 70 140 rsv rsv rsv rsv rsv

\index{e1000\+\_\+set\+\_\+d0\+\_\+lplu\+\_\+state\+\_\+82575@{e1000\+\_\+set\+\_\+d0\+\_\+lplu\+\_\+state\+\_\+82575}!e1000\+\_\+82575.\+c@{e1000\+\_\+82575.\+c}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{e1000\+\_\+set\+\_\+d0\+\_\+lplu\+\_\+state\+\_\+82575(struct e1000\+\_\+hw $\ast$hw, bool active)}{e1000_set_d0_lplu_state_82575(struct e1000_hw *hw, bool active)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}static {\bf s32} e1000\+\_\+set\+\_\+d0\+\_\+lplu\+\_\+state\+\_\+82575 (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}

\item[{{\bf bool}}]{active}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}\hypertarget{e1000__82575_8c_a775e190473572389844eaf331f5ec0fc}{}\label{e1000__82575_8c_a775e190473572389844eaf331f5ec0fc}
e1000\+\_\+set\+\_\+d0\+\_\+lplu\+\_\+state\+\_\+82575 -\/ Set Low Power Linkup D0 state \+: pointer to the HW structure \+: true to enable L\+P\+LU, false to disable

Sets the L\+P\+LU D0 state according to the active flag. When activating L\+P\+LU this function also disables smart speed and vice versa. L\+P\+LU will not be activated unless the device autonegotiation advertisement meets standards of either 10 or 10/100 or 10/100/1000 at all duplexes. This is a function pointer entry point only called by P\+HY setup routines.

\index{e1000\+\_\+set\+\_\+d3\+\_\+lplu\+\_\+state\+\_\+82580@{e1000\+\_\+set\+\_\+d3\+\_\+lplu\+\_\+state\+\_\+82580}!e1000\+\_\+82575.\+c@{e1000\+\_\+82575.\+c}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{e1000\+\_\+set\+\_\+d3\+\_\+lplu\+\_\+state\+\_\+82580(struct e1000\+\_\+hw $\ast$hw, bool active)}{e1000_set_d3_lplu_state_82580(struct e1000_hw *hw, bool active)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf s32} e1000\+\_\+set\+\_\+d3\+\_\+lplu\+\_\+state\+\_\+82580 (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{struct {\bf e1000\+\_\+hw} $\ast$}]{hw, }
\item[{{\bf bool}}]{active}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}\hypertarget{e1000__82575_8c_ad5269bea0b754b8fb54a8be8b936b85e}{}\label{e1000__82575_8c_ad5269bea0b754b8fb54a8be8b936b85e}
e1000\+\_\+set\+\_\+d3\+\_\+lplu\+\_\+state\+\_\+82580 -\/ Sets low power link up state for D3 \+: pointer to the HW structure \+: boolean used to enable/disable lplu

Success returns 0, Failure returns 1

The low power link up (lplu) state is set to the power management level D3 and Smart\+Speed is disabled when active is true, else clear lplu for D3 and enable Smartspeed. L\+P\+LU and Smartspeed are mutually exclusive. L\+P\+LU is used during Dx states where the power conservation is most important. During driver activity, Smart\+Speed should be enabled so performance is maintained. 

e1000\+\_\+82575.\+c 파일의 935 번째 라인에서 정의되었습니다.

\index{e1000\+\_\+82575.\+c@{e1000\+\_\+82575.\+c}!e1000\+\_\+set\+\_\+pcie\+\_\+completion\+\_\+timeout@{e1000\+\_\+set\+\_\+pcie\+\_\+completion\+\_\+timeout}}
\index{e1000\+\_\+set\+\_\+pcie\+\_\+completion\+\_\+timeout@{e1000\+\_\+set\+\_\+pcie\+\_\+completion\+\_\+timeout}!e1000\+\_\+82575.\+c@{e1000\+\_\+82575.\+c}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{e1000\+\_\+set\+\_\+pcie\+\_\+completion\+\_\+timeout(struct e1000\+\_\+hw $\ast$hw)}{e1000_set_pcie_completion_timeout(struct e1000_hw *hw)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}static {\bf s32} e1000\+\_\+set\+\_\+pcie\+\_\+completion\+\_\+timeout (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{struct {\bf e1000\+\_\+hw} $\ast$}]{hw}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}\hypertarget{e1000__82575_8c_a0cc9f664c5fdc0d2ee379d3dce62436a}{}\label{e1000__82575_8c_a0cc9f664c5fdc0d2ee379d3dce62436a}
e1000\+\_\+set\+\_\+pcie\+\_\+completion\+\_\+timeout -\/ set pci-\/e completion timeout \+: pointer to the HW structure

The defaults for 82575 and 82576 should be in the range of 50us to 50ms, however the hardware default for these parts is 500us to 1ms which is less than the 10ms recommended by the pci-\/e spec. To address this we need to increase the value to either 10ms to 200ms for capability version 1 config, or 16ms to 55ms for version 2. 

e1000\+\_\+82575.\+c 파일의 2224 번째 라인에서 정의되었습니다.

e1000\+\_\+setup\+\_\+copper\+\_\+link\+\_\+82575 -\/ Configure copper link settings \+: pointer to the HW structure

Configures the link for auto-\/neg or forced speed and duplex. Then we check for link, once link is established calls to configure collision distance and flow control are called.

\begin{DoxyParamCaption}

\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}\hypertarget{e1000__82575_8c_a9b372cd6a64b99c40168c63ce412e220}{}\label{e1000__82575_8c_a9b372cd6a64b99c40168c63ce412e220}
e1000\+\_\+setup\+\_\+serdes\+\_\+link\+\_\+82575 -\/ Setup link for serdes \+: pointer to the HW structure

Configure the physical coding sub-\/layer (P\+CS) link. The P\+CS link is used on copper connections where the serialized gigabit media independent interface (sgmii), or serdes fiber is being used. Configures the link for auto-\/negotiation or forces speed/duplex.

e1000\+\_\+sgmii\+\_\+active\+\_\+82575 -\/ Return sgmii state \+: pointer to the HW structure

82575 silicon has a serialized gigabit media independent interface (sgmii) which can be enabled for use in the embedded applications. Simply return the current state of the sgmii interface.

e1000\+\_\+sgmii\+\_\+uses\+\_\+mdio\+\_\+82575 -\/ Determine if I2C pins are for external M\+D\+IO \+: pointer to the HW structure

Called to determine if the I2C pins are being used for I2C or as an external M\+D\+IO interface since the two options are mutually exclusive.

e1000\+\_\+validate\+\_\+nvm\+\_\+checksum\+\_\+82580 -\/ Validate E\+E\+P\+R\+OM checksum \+: pointer to the HW structure

Calculates the E\+E\+P\+R\+OM section checksum by reading/adding each word of the E\+E\+P\+R\+OM and then verifies that the sum of the E\+E\+P\+R\+OM is equal to 0x\+B\+A\+BA.
